# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka Streams DSL to Processor API Migration

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the Kafka Streams DSL (map, filter, groupBy) and their corresponding Processor API equivalents, to support a team migrating from DSL to lower-level Processor API for custom state store management.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

```json
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

I've identified **15 key Java source files** in apache/kafka that implement the DSL and Processor API relationship:

### **DSL Layer** (High-level abstraction):
- **KStreamImpl** - Implements KStream DSL methods: filter, map, mapValues, groupBy, groupByKey
- **KTableImpl** - Implements KTable DSL operations with changelog semantics
- **KGroupedStreamImpl** - Handles results of groupBy for aggregation

### **Processor API Layer** (Low-level implementation):
1. **KStreamFilter** - Filter processor using FixedKeyProcessorSupplier
2. **KStreamMap** - Transform keys and values using ProcessorSupplier
3. **KStreamMapValues** - Transform values only using FixedKeyProcessorSupplier
4. **KStreamFlatMap** & **KStreamFlatMapValues** - Produce multiple outputs
5. **KTableFilter** - KTable filter with state store management
6. **KTableMapValues** - KTable value transformation with state store support
7. **KStreamAggregate** - Aggregation processor for groupBy results

### **Key Pattern**:
Each DSL method creates a `ProcessorParameters` with a corresponding `ProcessorSupplier`, which implements the actual transformation logic. For example:
- `KStreamImpl.filter()` → creates `KStreamFilter` processor
- `KStreamImpl.map()` → creates `KStreamMap` processor
- `KStreamImpl.groupBy()` → creates `KGroupedStreamImpl` → uses `KStreamAggregate`

This architecture allows teams to migrate from the convenience of DSL to direct Processor API control for custom state store management.

Each DSL operation is backed by a ProcessorSupplier that creates Processor instances:\\n\\n### KStream Processors:\\n\\n1. **KStreamFilter** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java)\\n   - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>\\n   - Implements the Predicate logic for filtering records\\n   - Inner class KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n\\n2. **KStreamMap** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java)\\n   - Implements ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>\\n   - Applies KeyValueMapper to transform both keys and values\\n   - Inner class KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n   - Accesses the Processor API context() to forward transformed records\\n\\n3. **KStreamMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMapValues.java)\\n   - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>\\n   - Applies ValueMapperWithKey to transform only values\\n   - Inner class KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n   - Uses FixedKeyRecord for records with unchanged keys\\n\\n4. **KStreamFlatMap** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMap.java)\\n   - Similar pattern to KStreamMap but produces multiple output records per input\\n\\n5. **KStreamFlatMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMapValues.java)\\n   - Similar pattern to KStreamMapValues but produces multiple output records\\n\\n### KTable Processors:\\n\\n1. **KTableFilter** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableFilter.java)\\n   - Implements KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>\\n   - Processes Change<VIn> records (changelog entries)\\n   - Handles state store management for materialized views\\n   - Inner class KTableFilterProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VIn>>\\n\\n2. **KTableMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableMapValues.java)\\n   - Implements KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>\\n   - Processes Change records with state store support\\n   - Handles both old and new values for changelog semantics\\n   - Inner class KTableMapValuesProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VOut>>\\n\\n### Aggregation Processors:\\n\\n1. **KStreamAggregate** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamAggregate.java)\\n   - Implements KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>\\n   - Used by KGroupedStream for aggregation operations\\n   - Manages state stores for accumulating aggregate values\\n   - Inner class KStreamAggregateProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n   - Processes records and maintains aggregate state\\n\\n## Integration Pattern\\n\\nThe migration pattern from DSL to Processor API follows this flow:\\n\\n1. DSL method call (e.g., `stream.filter(predicate)`) in KStreamImpl\\n2. Creates a ProcessorParameters with the corresponding Processor supplier\\n3. Processor supplier (e.g., KStreamFilter) implements ProcessorSupplier interface\\n4. Processor supplier's `get()` method returns a Processor instance\\n5. The Processor implements the actual logic, accessing ProcessorContext for:\\n   - Forwarding records downstream: `context().forward(record)`\\n   - Accessing state stores (for stateful operations)\\n   - Managing timestamps and metadata\\n\\n## Key Processor API Interfaces:\\n\\n- **ProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/ProcessorSupplier.java) - Factory for creating Processor instances\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java) - Specialized supplier for fixed-key operations\\n- **Processor** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Processor.java) - Base interface for all processors\\n- **FixedKeyProcessor** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessor.java) - Specialized processor for operations that don't change keys\\n\\nTeams migrating from DSL to Processor API can leverage these implementations as reference patterns for custom state store management, replacing the DSL convenience with direct Processor API control over store initialization, record processing, and forwarding logic.\"\n}\n",

This separation is essential for teams migrating from the DSL to the Processor API for custom state store management.\\n\\n## DSL Layer\\n\\nThe primary DSL implementation classes are:\\n\\n1. **KStreamImpl** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java) - The core implementation of the KStream DSL interface. Key DSL methods include:\\n   - `filter(Predicate)` - Filters records based on a predicate\\n   - `map(KeyValueMapper)` - Transforms both keys and values\\n   - `mapValues(ValueMapperWithKey)` - Transforms only values\\n   - `groupBy(KeyValueMapper)` - Groups records by a new key\\n   - `groupByKey()` - Groups records by their existing key\\n\\n2. **KTableImpl** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableImpl.java) - The implementation of the KTable (changelog stream) DSL interface with similar operations optimized for changelog semantics.\\n\\n3. **KGroupedStreamImpl** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KGroupedStreamImpl.java) - The implementation of KGroupedStream, representing the result of groupBy operations. It provides aggregation methods like `reduce()`, `count()`, and `aggregate()`.\\n\\n## Processor API Layer\\n\\nThe Processor API provides the low-level implementation details. Each DSL operation is backed by a ProcessorSupplier that creates Processor instances:\\n\\n### KStream Processors:\\n\\n1. **KStreamFilter** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java)\\n   - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>\\n   - Implements the Predicate logic for filtering records\\n   - Inner class KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n\\n2. **KStreamMap** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java)\\n   - Implements ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>\\n   - Applies KeyValueMapper to transform both keys and values\\n   - Inner class KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n   - Accesses the Processor API context() to forward transformed records\\n\\n3. **KStreamMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMapValues.java)\\n   - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>\\n   - Applies ValueMapperWithKey to transform only values\\n   - Inner class KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n   - Uses FixedKeyRecord for records with unchanged keys\\n\\n4. **KStreamFlatMap** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMap.java)\\n   - Similar pattern to KStreamMap but produces multiple output records per input\\n\\n5. **KStreamFlatMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMapValues.java)\\n   - Similar pattern to KStreamMapValues but produces multiple output records\\n\\n### KTable Processors:\\n\\n1. **KTableFilter** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableFilter.java)\\n   - Implements KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>\\n   - Processes Change<VIn> records (changelog entries)\\n   - Handles state store management for materialized views\\n   - Inner class KTableFilterProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VIn>>\\n\\n2. **KTableMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableMapValues.java)\\n   - Implements KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>\\n   - Processes Change records with state store support\\n   - Handles both old and new values for changelog semantics\\n   - Inner class KTableMapValuesProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VOut>>\\n\\n### Aggregation Processors:\\n\\n1. **KStreamAggregate** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamAggregate.java)\\n   - Implements KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>\\n   - Used by KGroupedStream for aggregation operations\\n   - Manages state stores for accumulating aggregate values\\n   - Inner class KStreamAggregateProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n   - Processes records and maintains aggregate state\\n\\n## Integration Pattern\\n\\nThe migration pattern from DSL to Processor API follows this flow:\\n\\n1. DSL method call (e.g., `stream.filter(predicate)`) in KStreamImpl\\n2. Creates a ProcessorParameters with the corresponding Processor supplier\\n3. Processor supplier (e.g., KStreamFilter) implements ProcessorSupplier interface\\n4. Processor supplier's `get()` method returns a Processor instance\\n5. The Processor implements the actual logic, accessing ProcessorContext for:\\n   - Forwarding records downstream: `context().forward(record)`\\n   - Accessing state stores (for stateful operations)\\n   - Managing timestamps and metadata\\n\\n## Key Processor API Interfaces:\\n\\n- **ProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/ProcessorSupplier.java) - Factory for creating Processor instances\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java) - Specialized supplier for fixed-key operations\\n- **Processor** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Processor.java) - Base interface for all processors\\n- **FixedKeyProcessor** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessor.java) - Specialized processor for operations that don't change keys\\n\\nTeams migrating from DSL to Processor API can leverage these implementations as reference patterns for custom state store management, replacing the DSL convenience with direct Processor API control over store initialization, record processing, and forwarding logic.\"\n}\n",
